恃其便以敖予,shi'qi'bian'yi'ao'yu
识其不可,shi'qi'bu'ke
是其才之美者也,shi'qi'cai'zhi'mei'zhe'ye
是其尘垢,shi'qi'chen'gou
是其尘垢粃糠,shi'qi'chen'gou'bi'kang
事其大夫之贤者,shi'qi'dai'fu'zhi'xian'zhe
是欺德也,shi'qi'de'ye
视其后者而鞭之,shi'qi'hou'zhe'er'bian'zhi
世蕲乎乱,shi'qi'hu'luan
事齐乎事楚乎,shi'qi'hu'shi'chu'hu
时其饥饱,shi'qi'ji'bao
使其君内热发于背,shi'qi'jun'nei're'fa'yu'bei
弑其君者,shi'qi'jun'zhe
失其民也,shi'qi'min'ye
失其民者,shi'qi'min'zhe
使齐人传之,shi'qi'ren'chuan'zhi
失其身而能事其亲者,shi'qi'shen'er'neng'shi'qi'qin'zhe
是其市南宜僚邪,shi'qi'shi'nan'yi'liao'xie
是其始死也,shi'qi'shi'si'ye
恃其所不,shi'qi'suo'bu
恃其所不知而后知天之所谓也,shi'qi'suo'bu'zhi'er'hou'zhi'tian'zhi'suo'wei'ye
是其所美者为神奇,shi'qi'suo'mei'zhe'wei'shen'qi
失其所谓,shi'qi'suo'wei
视其所以,shi'qi'suo'yi
是其所以为灵公也,shi'qi'suo'yi'wei'ling'gong'ye
十七为君妇,shi'qi'wei'jun'fu
使契为司徒,shi'qi'wei'si'tu
失其心也,shi'qi'xin'ye
是其言也,shi'qi'yan'ye
十七遗汝嫁,shi'qi'yi'ru'jia
是其于辩也,shi'qi'yu'bian'ye
使其子九男事之,shi'qi'zi'jiu'nan'shi'zhi
适千里者,shi'qian'li'zhe
是妾断肠时,shi'qie'duan'chang'shi
使秦复爱六国之人,shi'qin'fu'ai'liu'guo'zhi'ren
事亲弗悦,shi'qin'fu'yue
使秦穆公忘其贱,shi'qin'mu'gong'wang'qi'jian
是侵其德者也,shi'qin'qi'de'zhe'ye
事亲若曾子者,shi'qin'ruo'zeng'zi'zhe
事亲是也,shi'qin'shi'ye
是禽兽也,shi'qin'shou'ye
使亲忘我难,shi'qin'wang'wo'nan
使亲忘我易,shi'qin'wang'wo'yi
事亲为大,shi'qin'wei'da
时清独北还,shi'qing'du'bei'hai
世情恶衰歇,shi'qing'e'shuai'xie
史鳅奉御而进所,shi'qiu'feng'yu'er'jin'suo
是求马于唐肆也,shi'qiu'ma'yu'tang'si'ye
识秋娘庭院,shi'qiu'niang'ting'yuan
时取一醉,shi'qu'yi'zui
时人不识余心乐,shi'ren'bu'shi'yu'xin'le
矢人而耻为矢也,shi'ren'er'chi'wei'shi'ye
失仁而后义,shi'ren'er'hou'yi
世人解听不解赏,shi'ren'jie'ting'bu'jie'shang
使人乃以心服而不敢,shi'ren'nai'yi'xin'fu'er'bu'gan
矢人岂不仁於函人哉,shi'ren'qi'bu'ren'yu'han'ren'zai
使人求谕谌,shi'ren'qiu'yu'shen
使人授己国,shi'ren'shou'ji'guo
使人听此凋朱颜,shi'ren'ting'ci'diao'zhu'yan
矢人惟恐不伤人,shi'ren'wei'kong'bu'shang'ren
使人喜怒失位,shi'ren'xi'nu'shi'wei
是人也又请见,shi'ren'ye'you'qing'jian
使人以为己节,shi'ren'yi'wei'ji'jie
世人以形色名声为足以得彼之情,shi'ren'yi'xing'se'ming'sheng'wei'zu'yi'de'bi'zhi'qing
时人已知处,shi'ren'yi'zhi'chu
使人占之,shi'ren'zhan'zhi
是人这所恶也,shi'ren'zhe'suo'e'ye
适人之适,shi'ren'zhi'shi
适人之适而不自适其适者也,shi'ren'zhi'shi'er'bu'zi'shi'qi'shi'zhe'ye
是人之所同知也,shi'ren'zhi'suo'tong'zhi'ye
是人之所欲也,shi'ren'zhi'suo'yu'ye
是人之所知,shi'ren'zhi'suo'zhi
世人直为物逆旅耳,shi'ren'zhi'wei'wu'ni'lv'er
使人之意也消,shi'ren'zhi'yi'ye'xiao
市人之足,shi'ren'zhi'zu
十日而问,shi'ri'er'wen
时日害丧,shi'ri'hai'sang
十日寒之,shi'ri'han'zhi
十日九风雨,shi'ri'jiu'feng'yu
是日牵来赤墀下,shi'ri'qian'lai'chi'chi'xia
使日夜无隙,shi'ri'ye'wu'xi
十日又问,shi'ri'you'wen
十日自愁,shi'ri'zi'chou
仕如此其急也,shi'ru'ci'qi'ji'ye
事如芳草春长在,shi'ru'fang'cao'chun'zhang'zai
试入旧巢相并,shi'ru'jiu'chao'xiang'bing
试如是也,shi'ru'shi'ye
是入则亡,shi'ru'ze'wang
事若不成,shi'ruo'bu'cheng
是若果是也,shi'ruo'guo'shi'ye
视若营四海,shi'ruo'ying'si'hai
时靸双鸳响,shi'sa'shuang'yuan'xiang
诗三百篇,shi'san'bai'pian
十三教汝织,shi'san'jiao'ru'zhi
十三能织素,shi'san'neng'zhi'su
十三学得琵琶成,shi'san'xue'de'pi'pa'cheng
是三者虽异,shi'san'zhe'sui'yi
世丧道矣,shi'sang'dao'yi
视丧其足犹遗土也,shi'sang'qi'zu'you'yi'tu'ye
实丧易以危,shi'sang'yi'yi'wei
是色而已,shi'se'er'yi
十杀一人,shi'sha'yi'ren
是尚大不惑,shi'shang'da'bu'huo
世上功名,shi'shang'gong'ming
是上慢而残下也,shi'shang'man'er'can'xia'ye
世上荣枯无百年,shi'shang'rong'ku'wu'bai'nian
是尚为能充其类也乎,shi'shang'wei'neng'chong'qi'lei'ye'hu
世上未有如公贫,shi'shang'wei'you'ru'gong'pin
十觞亦不醉,shi'shang'yi'bu'zui
是尚友也,shi'shang'you'ye
是上与下同道,shi'shang'yu'xia'tong'dao
石上玉簪脆,shi'shang'yu'zan'cui
是社稷之臣也,shi'she'ji'zhi'chen'ye
是射之射,shi'she'zhi'she
十生九死到官所,shi'sheng'jiu'si'dao'guan'suo
使圣人多男子,shi'sheng'ren'duo'nan'zi
使圣人富,shi'sheng'ren'fu
是圣人仆也,shi'sheng'ren'pu'ye
使圣人寿,shi'sheng'ren'shou
世事波上舟,shi'shi'bo'shang'zhou
士师不能治士,shi'shi'bu'neng'zhi'shi
施施从外来,shi'shi'cong'wai'lai
世事蹉跎成白首,shi'shi'cuo'tuo'cheng'bai'shou
世事洞明皆学问,shi'shi'dong'ming'jie'xue'wen
室始洞然,shi'shi'dong'ran
适矢复沓,shi'shi'fu'ta
事事关心,shi'shi'guan'xin
始适还家门,shi'shi'hai'jia'men
十世可知也,shi'shi'ke'zhi'ye
世事空知学醉歌,shi'shi'kong'zhi'xue'zui'ge
是时孔子当,shi'shi'kong'zi'dang
世事两茫茫,shi'shi'liang'mang'mang
世事漫随流水,shi'shi'man'sui'liu'shui
世事茫茫难自料,shi'shi'mang'mang'nan'zi'liao
是使民养生丧死无憾也,shi'shi'min'yang'sheng'sang'si'wu'han'ye
适适然惊,shi'shi'ran'jing
食豕如食人,shi'shi'ru'shi'ren
试使山东之国与陈涉度长絜大,shi'shi'shan'dong'zhi'guo'yu'chen'she'duo'chang'xie'da
时势适然,shi'shi'shi'ran
豕虱是也,shi'shi'shi'ye
事事四五通,shi'shi'si'wu'tong
始时所是,shi'shi'suo'shi
时时为安慰,shi'shi'wei'an'wei
是时为帝者也,shi'shi'wei'di'zhe'ye

始是新承恩泽时,shi'shi'xin'cheng'en'ze'shi
世世以洴澼絖为事,shi'shi'yi'ping'pi'kuang'wei'shi
时时犹唱,shi'shi'you'chang
是室远而,shi'shi'yuan'er
是事之变,shi'shi'zhi'bian
十室之邑,shi'shi'zhi'yi

世叔讨论之,shi'shu'tao'lun'zhi
事孰为大,shi'shu'wei'da

实熟则剥,shi'shu'ze'bo
世衰道微,shi'shuai'dao'wei
是谁秋到便凄凉,shi'shui'qiu'dao'bian'qi'liang
逝水移川,shi'shui'yi'chuan

视死忽如归,shi'si'hu'ru'gui
十四能裁衣,shi'si'neng'cai'yi
视死若生者,shi'si'ruo'sheng'zhe
十四万人齐解甲,shi'si'wan'ren'qi'jie'jia

十四为君妇,shi'si'wei'jun'fu
十四学裁衣,shi'si'xue'cai'yi

世俗之人,shi'su'zhi'ren

世俗之所谓知者,shi'su'zhi'suo'wei'zhi'zhe

是岁大旱,shi'sui'da'han
世虽贵之,shi'sui'gui'zhi
是随香趁烛,shi'sui'xiang'chen'zhu
